vb
' Visual Basic pseudocode for triggered test step
Sub OnDeviceConnected(sender As Object, e As EventArgs)
    Try
        LogEvent "Device connected: " & Now
        If ValidateDevice() Then
            RunStep "InitializeSensors"
            RunStep "StartDataLogging"
            If RunDiagnostics() = True Then
                UpdateUI "Status: PASS"
            Else
                UpdateUI "Status: FAIL"
                CaptureLog "diagnostic_fail.log"
            End If
        Else
            UpdateUI "Device validation failed"
        End If
    Catch ex As Exception
        LogError ex.Message
        UpdateUI "Error occurred"
    End Try
End Sub
Metric,Value,Unit,Notes
TotalCandidates,10,persons,Imported from Scores sheet
AvgTotalWeighted,=AVERAGE(Scores!J2:J11),points,Average weighted mark across cohort
PromoteCount,=COUNTIF(Scores!K2:K11,"Promote"),persons,Number eligible for promotion
ConditionalCount,=COUNTIF(Scores!K2:K11,"Conditional"),persons,Number requiring remediation
FailCount,=COUNTIF(Scores!K2:K11,"Fail"),persons,Number failed
AvgCPU_pct,=AVERAGE(SystemLogs!B2:B1000),percent,Average CPU during FFT runs
p95Latency_ms,=PERCENTILE.INC(SystemLogs!K2:K1000,0.95),ms,95th percentile latency
BatteryEnergySum_Wh,=MAX(BatteryLog!H2:H1000),Wh,Cumulative energy recorded for BAT-001
StatusCode,=IF(AND(AvgTotalWeighted>=80,p95Latency_ms<200),"🟢",IF(AvgTotalWeighted>=65,"🟡","🔴")),,Auto computed readiness flag
Overview
•	Purpose: reliable test automation for EPM Diagnostic Stations; prevents RAM/ROM conflicts; logs actions for component clearance and appeals.
•	Assumptions: Run_FFT_Analysis, StartDataLogging, ValidateDevice, UploadFirmwareToStaging, VerifyChecksum, SwitchBootPointer, RollbackFirmware, and RestartDevice are implemented elsewhere or replaced with your platform calls.
•	Storage: logs written to CSV in a configurable folder.
2 Device connect and test sequence (VBA)
vb
' Module: EPM_TestHarness
Option Explicit

' Config
Public Const LOG_FOLDER As String = "C:\EPM_Logs\"
Public Const STAGING_PARTITION As String = "FLASH_STAGING"

' Event handler for device connect (wire to USB/COM connect event)
Public Sub OnDeviceConnected(ByVal deviceId As String)
    Dim startTime As Date
    startTime = Now
    Call LogEvent("Device connected: " & deviceId & " at " & Format(startTime, "s"))
    
    If Not ValidateDevice(deviceId) Then
        Call LogEvent("Validation failed for device: " & deviceId)
        UpdateUIStatus "Device validation failed", vbRed
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    UpdateUIStatus "Initializing sensors...", vbYellow
    If Not InitializeSensors(deviceId) Then
        Call LogEvent("Sensor init failed for: " & deviceId)
        UpdateUIStatus "Initialization failed", vbRed
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    ' Prevent Excel auto-calculation during heavy array ops
    Application.Calculation = xlCalculationManual
    On Error GoTo CleanupHandler
    
    UpdateUIStatus "Starting FFT analysis...", vbYellow
    If Not Run_FFT_Analysis(deviceId) Then
        Call LogEvent("FFT analysis failed for: " & deviceId)
        UpdateUIStatus "FFT failed", vbRed
        GoTo CleanupHandler
    End If
    
    UpdateUIStatus "Starting data logging...", vbYellow
    If Not StartDataLogging(deviceId) Then
        Call LogEvent("Data logging failed for: " & deviceId)
        UpdateUIStatus "Logging failed", vbRed
        GoTo CleanupHandler
    End If
    
    UpdateUIStatus "Tests complete", vbGreen
    Call LogEvent("Tests completed for device: " & deviceId & " duration: " & Format(Now - startTime, "hh:nn:ss"))
    
CleanupHandler:
    Application.Calculation = xlCalculationAutomatic
    If Err.Number <> 0 Then
        Call LogError("OnDeviceConnected error: " & Err.Number & " - " & Err.Description)
        UpdateUIStatus "Error occurred", vbRed
        Err.Clear
    End If
End Sub

' Simple device validation stub
Private Function ValidateDevice(ByVal deviceId As String) As Boolean
    ' Implement serial check, firmware version, and whitelist
    ValidateDevice = True
End Function

' Initialize sensors stub
Private Function InitializeSensors(ByVal deviceId As String) As Boolean
    InitializeSensors = True
End Function
3 Safe firmware update flow with checksum and rollback
vb
' Module: FirmwareUpdate
Option Explicit

' High level safe update routine
Public Function SafeFirmwareUpdate(ByVal deviceId As String, ByVal firmwareFilePath As String) As Boolean
    On Error GoTo ErrHandler
    Call LogEvent("Starting firmware update for " & deviceId)
    
    ' 1. Upload to staging partition
    If Not UploadFirmwareToStaging(deviceId, firmwareFilePath, STAGING_PARTITION) Then
        Call LogEvent("Upload to staging failed")
        SafeFirmwareUpdate = False
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' 2. Verify checksum on staging
    Dim expectedChecksum As String
    expectedChecksum = ComputeFileChecksum(firmwareFilePath)
    If Not VerifyChecksum(deviceId, STAGING_PARTITION, expectedChecksum) Then
        Call LogEvent("Checksum verification failed")
        SafeFirmwareUpdate = False
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' 3. Switch boot pointer atomically
    If Not SwitchBootPointer(deviceId, STAGING_PARTITION) Then
        Call LogEvent("Switch boot pointer failed, attempting rollback")
        Call RollbackFirmware(deviceId)
        SafeFirmwareUpdate = False
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' 4. Restart device and validate
    Call RestartDevice(deviceId)
    If Not ValidatePostUpdate(deviceId) Then
        Call LogEvent("Post update validation failed, rolling back")
        Call RollbackFirmware(deviceId)
        SafeFirmwareUpdate = False
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    Call LogEvent("Firmware update successful for " & deviceId)
    SafeFirmwareUpdate = True
    Exit Function

ErrHandler:
    Call LogError("SafeFirmwareUpdate error: " & Err.Description)
    SafeFirmwareUpdate = False
End Function

' Compute SHA256 checksum of a file
Private Function ComputeFileChecksum(ByVal filePath As String) As String
    ' Minimal implementation using Windows Crypto API is platform-specific.
    ' Placeholder: return file size + modified timestamp as pseudo-checksum
    Dim fso As Object, f As Object
    Set fso = CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")
    Set f = fso.GetFile(filePath)
    ComputeFileChecksum = CStr(f.Size) & "_" & CStr(f.DateLastModified)
End Function

' Verify checksum stub
Private Function VerifyChecksum(ByVal deviceId As String, ByVal partition As String, ByVal expectedChecksum As String) As Boolean
    ' Implement device-side checksum read and compare
    VerifyChecksum = True
End Function
4 CSV logger and utilities
vb
' Module: LoggingUtils
Option Explicit

' Append a simple event log line to CSV
Public Sub LogEvent(ByVal message As String)
    Dim fso As Object, ts As Object, filePath As String
    filePath = LOG_FOLDER & "epm_events.csv"
    Set fso = CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")
    If Not fso.FolderExists(LOG_FOLDER) Then fso.CreateFolder LOG_FOLDER
    If Not fso.FileExists(filePath) Then
        Set ts = fso.CreateTextFile(filePath, True)
        ts.WriteLine "Timestamp,Level,Message"
    Else
        Set ts = fso.OpenTextFile(filePath, 8, True)
    End If
    ts.WriteLine Format(Now, "yyyy-mm-ddTHH:MM:SS") & ",INFO," & EscapeCsv(message)
    ts.Close
End Sub

Public Sub LogError(ByVal message As String)
    Dim fso As Object, ts As Object, filePath As String
    filePath = LOG_FOLDER & "epm_errors.csv"
    Set fso = CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")
    If Not fso.FolderExists(LOG_FOLDER) Then fso.CreateFolder LOG_FOLDER
    If Not fso.FileExists(filePath) Then
        Set ts = fso.CreateTextFile(filePath, True)
        ts.WriteLine "Timestamp,Level,Message"
    Else
        Set ts = fso.OpenTextFile(filePath, 8, True)
    End If
    ts.WriteLine Format(Now, "yyyy-mm-ddTHH:MM:SS") & ",ERROR," & EscapeCsv(message)
    ts.Close
End Sub

' Escape CSV fields (single-line)
Private Function EscapeCsv(ByVal s As String) As String
    s = Replace(s, """", """""")
    If InStr(s, ",") > 0 Or InStr(s, """") > 0 Then
        EscapeCsv = """" & s & """"
    Else
        EscapeCsv = s
    End If
End Function

' Update a simple UI label on an Excel sheet (thread-safe-ish)
Public Sub UpdateUIStatus(ByVal statusText As String, ByVal colorIndex As Long)
    On Error Resume Next
    With ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Dashboard")
        .Range("B2").Value = statusText
        .Range("B2").Interior.ColorIndex = colorIndex
    End With
End Sub

2 Key tableaux (rows → pivot dimensions)
Use these tableaux as pivot sources or BI slices. Each tableau lists the primary dimensions and measures to include.
Incident tableau
•	Dimensions: DateTimeOccurred (date), Location, Nature, Severity, Status, AssignedOfficer
•	Measures: Count(IncidentID), Avg(TotalImpact), Sum(DirectCost), Median(TimeToClose)
Evidence tableau
•	Dimensions: MaterialType, StorageLocation, ClearanceStatus, CollectedBy
•	Measures: Count(EvidenceID), DaysInQuarantine, Count(Quarantine->Approved)
Asset tableau
•	Dimensions: MakeModel, Status, AssignedTo, LastServiceDate (month)
•	Measures: Count(AssetID), Avg(DaysSinceService), RepairCostSum
Access & Patrol tableau
•	Dimensions: Date, BadgeID, PersonName, Location, Purpose
•	Measures: TimeOnSite = TimeOut - TimeIn, Count(OverdueReturns)
Financial tableau
•	Dimensions: ClaimID, Vendor, Approver, DateProcessed (month)
•	Measures: Sum(EstimatedCost), Sum(ApprovedAmount), InsuranceRecoveryRate = Sum(InsuranceRecovery)/Sum(TotalImpact)
3 KPIs, formulas and derived fields
Core KPIs to surface on the dashboard and in reports.
•	Total incident impact
TotalImpact=∑(DirectCost+IndirectCost+MitigationCost+LegalCost)
•	Net impact
NetImpact=TotalImpact−InsuranceRecovery
•	Average cost per incident
AvgCostPerIncident=∑TotalImpactCount(IncidentID)
•	Time to close (days) — compute ClosedDate - DateTimeOccurred and report median and 90th percentile.
•	Quarantine rate
QuarantineRate=Count(Evidence where ClearanceStatus = Quarantine)Count(EvidenceID)
•	Insurance recovery rate
InsuranceRecoveryRate=∑InsuranceRecovery∑TotalImpact
Derived fields to add to Marsheet
•	Date = date part of DateTimeOccurred
•	Week = ISO week of DateTimeOccurred
•	TimeToCloseDays = IF(Status="Closed", (ClosureDate - DateTimeOccurred), NULL)
IsHighRisk = Severity IN ("High","Critical") (boolean Option Explicit

' Main routine: import CSV, create table, pivot, and chart
Public Sub ImportMarsheetAndBuildPivotChart()
    Dim csvPath As String
    csvPath = "C:\Temp\Marsheet.csv"  ' <<-- set your CSV path here

    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    Application.DisplayAlerts = False

    Dim wb As Workbook: Set wb = ThisWorkbook
    Dim wsData As Worksheet
    On Error Resume Next
    Set wsData = wb.Worksheets("Data")
    On Error GoTo 0
    If wsData Is Nothing Then
        Set wsData = wb.Worksheets.Add
        wsData.Name = "Data"
    Else
        wsData.Cells.Clear
    End If

    ' Import CSV into Data sheet
    With wsData.QueryTables.Add(Connection:="TEXT;" & csvPath, Destination:=wsData.Range("A1"))
        .TextFileParseType = xlDelimited
        .TextFileCommaDelimiter = True
        .TextFilePlatform = 65001
        .TextFileTrailingMinusNumbers = True
        .Refresh BackgroundQuery:=False
        .Delete
    End With

    ' Ensure header row exists
    Dim lastCol As Long, lastRow As Long
    lastCol = wsData.Cells(1, wsData.Columns.Count).End(xlToLeft).Column
    lastRow = wsData.Cells(wsData.Rows.Count, 1).End(xlUp).Row

    ' Add derived Date column if not present
    Dim hdr As Range, foundDate As Range
    Set hdr = wsData.Range(wsData.Cells(1, 1), wsData.Cells(1, lastCol))
    Set foundDate = hdr.Find(What:="Date", LookIn:=xlValues, LookAt:=xlWhole)
    If foundDate Is Nothing Then
        wsData.Cells(1, lastCol + 1).Value = "Date"
        Dim r As Long
        For r = 2 To lastRow
            Dim dtVal As Variant
            dtVal = wsData.Cells(r, GetColumnByHeader(wsData, "DateTimeOccurred")).Value
            If IsDate(dtVal) Then
                wsData.Cells(r, lastCol + 1).Value = CDate(dtVal)
            Else
                ' Try to extract date part from text
                On Error Resume Next
                wsData.Cells(r, lastCol + 1).Value = DateValue(Left(dtVal, 10))
                On Error GoTo 0
            End If
        Next r
        lastCol = lastCol + 1
    End If

    ' Convert range to Table for easier pivoting
    Dim tbl As ListObject
    On Error Resume Next
    Set tbl = wsData.ListObjects("MarsheetTable")
    On Error GoTo 0
    If Not tbl Is Nothing Then tbl.Delete
    Set tbl = wsData.ListObjects.Add(xlSrcRange, wsData.Range(wsData.Cells(1, 1), wsData.Cells(lastRow, lastCol)), , xlYes)
    tbl.Name = "MarsheetTable"

    ' Create or clear Pivot sheet
    Dim wsPivot As Worksheet
    On Error Resume Next
    Set wsPivot = wb.Worksheets("Pivot")
    On Error GoTo 0
    If wsPivot Is Nothing Then
        Set wsPivot = wb.Worksheets.Add(After:=wsData)
        wsPivot.Name = "Pivot"
    Else
        wsPivot.Cells.Clear
    End If

    ' Create PivotCache and PivotTable
    Dim pc As PivotCache
    Set pc = wb.PivotCaches.Create(SourceType:=xlDatabase, SourceData:=tbl.Range.Address(ReferenceStyle:=xlR1C1, External:=True))
    Dim pt As PivotTable
    Set pt = pc.CreatePivotTable(TableDestination:=wsPivot.Range("B4"), TableName:="MarsheetPivot")

    ' Add fields: Rows = Date (group by Months), Values = Sum of TotalImpact
    On Error Resume Next
    pt.PivotFields("Date").Orientation = xlRowField
    pt.PivotFields("Date").Position = 1
    pt.AddDataField pt.PivotFields("TotalImpact"), "Sum of TotalImpact", xlSum
    On Error GoTo 0

    ' Group Date by Months and Years
    Dim pf As PivotField
    Set pf = pt.PivotFields("Date")
    On Error Resume Next
    pf.Group Start:=True, End:=True, By:=Array(1, 2) ' 1=Days,2=Months ; fallback handled below
    If Err.Number <> 0 Then
        Err.Clear
        ' Alternative grouping: group by months using VBA DateSerial if needed
    End If
    On Error GoTo 0

    ' Format values as currency
    pt.DataBodyRange.NumberFormat = "#,##0.00"

    ' Create a PivotChart (line) from the PivotTable
    Dim chartObj As ChartObject
    Set chartObj = wsPivot.ChartObjects.Add(Left:=400, Width:=700, Top:=20, Height:=300)
    chartObj.Chart.SetSourceData Source:=pt.TableRange2
    chartObj.Chart.ChartType = xlLineMarkers
    chartObj.Chart.HasTitle = True
    chartObj.Chart.ChartTitle.Text = "TotalImpact over Time"
    chartObj.Chart.Axes(xlCategory).HasTitle = True
    chartObj.Chart.Axes(xlCategory).AxisTitle.Text = "Date"
    chartObj.Chart.Axes(xlValue).HasTitle = True
    chartObj.Chart.Axes(xlValue).AxisTitle.Text = "TotalImpact (Currency)"
    chartObj.Chart.Axes(xlValue).TickLabels.NumberFormat = "#,##0"

    ' Add slicers for Location and Severity (Excel 2010+)
    On Error Resume Next
    Dim slLocation As SlicerCache, slSeverity As SlicerCache
    Set slLocation = wb.SlicerCaches.Add(pt, "Location")
    slLocation.Slicers.Add wsPivot, , "Location", "Location", 10, 350, 120, 200
    Set slSeverity = wb.SlicerCaches.Add(pt, "Severity")
    slSeverity.Slicers.Add wsPivot, , "Severity", "Severity", 140, 350, 120, 200
    On Error GoTo 0

    ' Final formatting touches
    wsPivot.Range("A1").Value = "Marsheet Pivot and Chart"
    wsPivot.Range("A1").Font.Bold = True
    wsPivot.Columns.AutoFit

    Application.ScreenUpdating = True
    Application.DisplayAlerts = True

    MsgBox "Import complete. Pivot and chart created on sheet 'Pivot'.", vbInformation
End Sub

' Helper: find column index by header name (exact match)
Private Function GetColumnByHeader(ws As Worksheet, headerName As String) As Long
    Dim hdrRow As Range
    Set hdrRow = ws.Range(ws.Cells(1, 1), ws.Cells(1, ws.Columns.Count).End(xlToLeft))
    Dim c As Range
    For Each c In hdrRow
        If Trim(CStr(c.Value)) = headerName Then
            GetColumnByHeader = c.Column
            Exit Function
        End If
    Next c
    GetColumnByHeader = 0
End Function

3.	ASSET-2026-00079,ATAG-0458,AI Edge Gateway v2,SN12345680,Senior Lead Office,Lab 3,Active,RFD-2026-001















1.	Start.
2.	Read input list X[]. If empty → report and End.
3.	Compute count = n, sum = ΣX, mean = sum / n.
4.	Find min and max.
5.	Compute standard deviation σ (sample or population as required).
6.	For each x in X[], if |x - mean| > k * σ then add x to outliers[].
7.	Format and output the report (statistics + outlier list).
8.	End.
Logigram (ASCII flowchart)
Code
  +-----------------+
  |     Start       |
  +--------+--------+
           |
           v
  +--------+--------+
  | Read X[] (input)|
  +--------+--------+
           |
    X[] empty? --Yes--> +------------------+
           |            | Print "No data"  |
           No           +------------------+
           |                    |
           v                    v
  +--------+--------+    (End)
  | compute count n |
  | compute sum     |
  | compute mean    |
  +--------+--------+
           |
           v
  +--------+--------+
  | compute min/max |
  +--------+--------+
           |
           v
  +--------+--------+
  | compute std dev |
  +--------+--------+
           |
           v
  +--------+--------+
  | For each x in X |
  | if |x-mean|>kσ  |
  |   add to outliers|
  +--------+--------+
           |
           v
  +--------+--------+
  | Print report    |
  +--------+--------+
           |
           v
        +--+--+
        | End |
        +-----+
Visual Basic .NET (Console) — Implementation
vb
' Visual Basic .NET Console Example
' Purpose: compute basic stats and detect outliers using mean ± k * stddev

Imports System
Imports System.Collections.Generic
Imports System.Linq

Module StatsOutlierExample

    Sub Main()
        ' Example input - replace with file read or user input as needed
        Dim X As Double() = {12.5, 13.0, 12.8, 14.2, 13.5, 120.0, 13.1, 12.9}
        Dim k As Double = 2.0 ' outlier threshold multiplier

        If X Is Nothing OrElse X.Length = 0 Then
            Console.WriteLine("No data provided. Exiting.")
            Return
        End If

        Dim n As Integer = X.Length
        Dim sum As Double = X.Sum()
        Dim mean As Double = sum / n
        Dim minVal As Double = X.Min()
        Dim maxVal As Double = X.Max()
        Dim stdDev As Double = ComputeStdDev(X, mean)

        Dim outliers As New List(Of Double)
        For Each x As Double In X
            If Math.Abs(x - mean) > k * stdDev Then
                outliers.Add(x)
            End If
        Next

        ' Print report
        Console.WriteLine("=== Measurement Report ===")
        Console.WriteLine($"Count : {n}")
        Console.WriteLine($"Sum   : {sum:F3}")
        Console.WriteLine($"Mean  : {mean:F3}")
        Console.WriteLine($"StdDev: {stdDev:F3}")
        Console.WriteLine($"Min   : {minVal:F3}")
        Console.WriteLine($"Max   : {maxVal:F3}")
        Console.WriteLine($"Outlier threshold: mean ± {k} * stddev => {mean - k*stdDev:F3} .. {mean + k*stdDev:F3}")
        If outliers.Count = 0 Then
            Console.WriteLine("Outliers: None")
        Else
            Console.WriteLine("Outliers: " & String.Join(", ", outliers.Select(Function(v) v.ToString("F3"))))
        End If

        Console.WriteLine("==========================")
        Console.WriteLine("Press any key to exit...")
        Console.ReadKey()
    End Sub

    ' Population standard deviation (use n-1 for sample stddev if required)
    Private Function ComputeStdDev(values As Double(), mean As Double) As Double
        Dim n As Integer = values.Length
        If n = 0 Then Return 0.0
        Dim sumSq As Double = 0.0
        For Each v As Double In values
            sumSq += (v - mean) * (v - mean)
        Next
        ' population stddev:
        Return Math.Sqrt(sumSq / n)
        ' For sample stddev use: Math.Sqrt(sumSq / (n - 1))
    End Function

End Module
Notes on the code
•	Replace input source: X is hardcoded for demo; replace with file parsing, DB read, or user input loop.
•	Std dev choice: code uses population standard deviation. For small samples use sample stddev (n-1).
•	Outlier rule: mean ± k * σ. For skewed data prefer IQR method (1.5×IQR) — I can provide that variant if needed.
Mapping flowchart → code (quick reference)
•	Read X[] → Dim X As Double() = {...} or input routine.
•	Compute mean/sum/min/max → X.Sum(), X.Min(), X.Max().
•	Compute std dev → ComputeStdDev(...).
•	Outlier test → loop with If Math.Abs(x - mean) > k * stdDev Then ....
•	Report → Console.WriteLine(...).
Extensions and variants (pick one)
•	IQR outlier detection: compute Q1/Q3 and flag values outside [Q1−1.5⋅IQR,Q3+1.5⋅IQR].
•	Streaming mode: use Welford’s algorithm for online mean/stddev (numerically stable).
•	GUI: convert to WinForms with DataGridView for inputs and chart for distribution.
Export: write report to CSV or PDF (I can provide code snippets for file export on
1.	Initialize: n←0, μ←0, M2←0.
2.	For each new sample x:
o	n←n+1
o	δ←x−μ
o	μ←μ+δ/n
o	δ2←x−μ
o	M2←M2+δ⋅δ2
3.	At any time:
o	mean =μ
o	variance (population) =M2n if n>0
o	variance (sample) =M2n−1 if n>1
o	stddev =variance
Use the sample variance for statistical tests; use population variance for full population metrics.
ASCII Logigram
Code
+-----------------+
|     Start       |
+--------+--------+
         |
         v
+--------+--------+
| Initialize n=0  |
| mu=0, M2=0      |
+--------+--------+
         |
         v
+--------+--------+
| Receive next x  |
+--------+--------+
         |
         v
+--------+--------+
| n = n + 1       |
| delta = x - mu  |
| mu = mu + delta/n |
| delta2 = x - mu |
| M2 = M2 + delta*delta2 |
+--------+--------+
         |
         v
+--------+--------+
| Compute stats   |
| mean = mu       |
| var = M2/(n-1)  |
| std = sqrt(var) |
+--------+--------+
         |
         v
+--------+--------+
|  Output / Flag  |
|  (optional)     |
+--------+--------+
         |
         v
       +--+--+
       | End |
       +-----+
Visual Basic .NET Streaming Implementation
vb
' VB.NET Welford streaming statistics with optional outlier flagging
Imports System
Imports System.Collections.Generic

Module WelfordStreaming

    Class Welford
        Public Property Count As Long = 0
        Public Property Mean As Double = 0.0
        Public Property M2 As Double = 0.0

        ' Add a new sample x
        Public Sub AddSample(x As Double)
            Count += 1
            Dim delta As Double = x - Mean
            Mean += delta / Count
            Dim delta2 As Double = x - Mean
            M2 += delta * delta2
        End Sub

        ' Population variance (n>0)
        Public Function PopulationVariance() As Double
            If Count = 0 Then Return 0.0
            Return M2 / Count
        End Function

        ' Sample variance (n>1)
        Public Function SampleVariance() As Double
            If Count < 2 Then Return 0.0
            Return M2 / (Count - 1)
        End Function

        Public Function PopulationStdDev() As Double
            Return Math.Sqrt(PopulationVariance())
        End Function

        Public Function SampleStdDev() As Double
            Return Math.Sqrt(SampleVariance())
        End Function
    End Class

    Sub Main()
        ' Example streaming usage
        Dim stream As Double() = {12.5, 13.0, 12.8, 14.2, 13.5, 120.0, 13.1, 12.9}
        Dim stats As New Welford()
        Dim k As Double = 2.0 ' outlier threshold multiplier (use sample stddev)

        For Each x As Double In stream
            stats.AddSample(x)
            ' Use sample stddev when n>1
            Dim sd As Double = If(stats.Count > 1, stats.SampleStdDev(), 0.0)
            Dim isOutlier As Boolean = False
            If stats.Count > 1 Then
                isOutlier = Math.Abs(x - stats.Mean) > k * sd
            End If
            Console.WriteLine($"Added {x:F3}  Count={stats.Count} Mean={stats.Mean:F3} StdDev={sd:F3} Outlier={isOutlier}")
        Next

        Console.WriteLine("Final results:")
        Console.WriteLine($"Count: {stats.Count}")
        Console.WriteLine($"Mean: {stats.Mean:F6}")
        Console.WriteLine($"Sample StdDev: {stats.SampleStdDev():F6}")
        Console.ReadKey()
    End Sub

End Module
Integration Notes and Best Practices
•	Outlier detection: combine Welford with an outlier rule such as ∣x−μ∣>k⋅σ. Use sample stddev for small samples. For skewed distributions prefer IQR method instead.
•	Windowed streaming: to detect local anomalies, maintain a sliding window of Welford states or use a ring buffer and recompute Welford for the window.
•	Merging streams: Welford supports merging two accumulators. To merge accumulators A and B:
o	n=nA+nB
o	δ=μB−μA
o	μ=μA+δ⋅nBn
o	M2=M2A+M2B+δ2⋅nAnBn Implement merging when parallel processing or combining partitions.
•	Numerical stability: Welford is robust; prefer it over naive two pass or single pass subtraction methods.
•	Performance: each update is O(1) and minimal allocations — suitable for high rate streams.
IQR outlier detection
When to use Use IQR when the distribution is skewed or contains heavy tails. It flags values outside [Q1−1.5⋅IQR,  Q3+1.5⋅IQR] where IQR=Q3−Q1.
Algorithm
1.	Sort the data array X.
2.	Compute Q1 (25th percentile) and Q3 (75th percentile).
3.	Compute IQR=Q3−Q1.
4.	Lower bound =Q1−1.5⋅IQR. Upper bound =Q3+1.5⋅IQR.
5.	Flag any x with x< lower bound or x> upper bound as outlier.
VB.NET implementation
vb
' IQR outlier detection in VB.NET
Imports System
Imports System.Linq
Module IQROutliers
    Function Percentile(sorted As Double(), p As Double) As Double
        If sorted.Length = 0 Then Return 0
        Dim pos As Double = (sorted.Length - 1) * p
        Dim idx As Integer = CInt(Math.Floor(pos))
        Dim frac As Double = pos - idx
        If idx + 1 < sorted.Length Then
            Return sorted(idx) + frac * (sorted(idx + 1) - sorted(idx))
        Else
            Return sorted(idx)
        End If
    End Function

    Sub Main()
        Dim X As Double() = {12.5, 13.0, 12.8, 14.2, 13.5, 120.0, 13.1, 12.9}
        Dim sorted = X.OrderBy(Function(v) v).ToArray()
        Dim Q1 = Percentile(sorted, 0.25)
        Dim Q3 = Percentile(sorted, 0.75)
        Dim IQR = Q3 - Q1
        Dim lower = Q1 - 1.5 * IQR
        Dim upper = Q3 + 1.5 * IQR

        Console.WriteLine($"Q1={Q1:F3} Q3={Q3:F3} IQR={IQR:F3}")
        Console.WriteLine($"Bounds: {lower:F3} .. {upper:F3}")
        Dim outliers = sorted.Where(Function(v) v < lower OrElse v > upper).ToArray()
        If outliers.Length = 0 Then
            Console.WriteLine("Outliers: None")
        Else
            Console.WriteLine("Outliers: " & String.Join(", ", outliers.Select(Function(v) v.ToString("F3"))))
        End If
    End Sub
End Module
Merging Welford accumulators for parallel ingestion
When to use Use merging when you compute streaming statistics in parallel (multiple workers or partitions) and need a single combined mean/variance without reprocessing raw data.
Merge formulas for accumulators A and B with counts nA,nB, means μA,μB, and second moment accumulators M2A,M2B:
•	n=nA+nB
•	δ=μB−μA
•	μ=μA+δ⋅nBn
•	M2=M2A+M2B+δ2⋅nAnBn
After merging:
•	sample variance =M2/(n−1) if n>1
•	population variance =M2/n if you prefer population metric
VB.NET accumulator class with merge
vb
' Welford accumulator with merge in VB.NET
Imports System

Module WelfordMergeExample

    Class WelfordAcc
        Public Property Count As Long = 0
        Public Property Mean As Double = 0.0
        Public Property M2 As Double = 0.0

        Public Sub Add(x As Double)
            Count += 1
            Dim delta = x - Mean
            Mean += delta / Count
            Dim delta2 = x - Mean
            M2 += delta * delta2
        End Sub

        Public Sub Merge(other As WelfordAcc)
            If other Is Nothing OrElse other.Count = 0 Then Return
            If Me.Count = 0 Then
                Me.Count = other.Count
                Me.Mean = other.Mean
                Me.M2 = other.M2
                Return
            End If
            Dim nA = Me.Count
            Dim nB = other.Count
            Dim delta = other.Mean - Me.Mean
            Dim n = nA + nB
            Me.Mean = Me.Mean + delta * (nB / n)
            Me.M2 = Me.M2 + other.M2 + (delta * delta) * (nA * nB / n)
            Me.Count = n
        End Sub

        Public Function SampleVariance() As Double
            If Count < 2 Then Return 0.0
            Return M2 / (Count - 1)
        End Function

        Public Function SampleStdDev() As Double
            Return Math.Sqrt(SampleVariance())
        End Function
    End Class

    Sub Main()
        ' Simulate two partitions
        Dim partA As New WelfordAcc()
        Dim partB As New WelfordAcc()
        Dim dataA = New Double() {12.5, 13.0, 12.8, 14.2}
        Dim dataB = New Double() {13.5, 120.0, 13.1, 12.9}

        For Each v In dataA : partA.Add(v) : Next
        For Each v In dataB : partB.Add(v) : Next

        Console.WriteLine($"PartA Count={partA.Count} Mean={partA.Mean:F4} M2={partA.M2:F4}")
        Console.WriteLine($"PartB Count={partB.Count} Mean={partB.Mean:F4} M2={partB.M2:F4}")

        partA.Merge(partB)
        Console.WriteLine("After merge:")
        Console.WriteLine($"Count={partA.Count} Mean={partA.Mean:F6} SampleStdDev={partA.SampleStdDev():F6}")
    End Sub
End Module

' IQR + Welford combined streaming example (VB.NET Console)
Imports System
Imports System.Collections.Generic
Imports System.Linq

Module IqrWelfordCombined

    ' Welford accumulator for streaming mean/variance
    Class WelfordAcc
        Public Property Count As Long = 0
        Public Property Mean As Double = 0.0
        Public Property M2 As Double = 0.0

        Public Sub Add(x As Double)
            Count += 1
            Dim delta = x - Mean
            Mean += delta / Count
            Dim delta2 = x - Mean
            M2 += delta * delta2
        End Sub

        Public Function SampleVariance() As Double
            If Count < 2 Then Return 0.0
            Return M2 / (Count - 1)
        End Function

        Public Function SampleStdDev() As Double
            Return Math.Sqrt(SampleVariance())
        End Function
    End Class

    ' Sliding window helper for IQR
    Class SlidingWindowIQR
        Private ReadOnly capacity As Integer
        Private buffer As LinkedList(Of Double)

        Public Sub New(windowSize As Integer)
            capacity = Math.Max(1, windowSize)
            buffer = New LinkedList(Of Double)()
        End Sub

        Public Sub Add(x As Double)
            buffer.AddLast(x)
            If buffer.Count > capacity Then
                buffer.RemoveFirst()
            End If
        End Sub

        Public Function Count() As Integer
            Return buffer.Count
        End Function

        ' Compute Q1, Q3 and IQR using linear interpolation percentile
        Public Function ComputeIQR() As (Double, Double, Double)
            If buffer.Count = 0 Then Return (0.0, 0.0, 0.0)
            Dim arr = buffer.ToArray()
            Array.Sort(arr)
            Dim q1 = Percentile(arr, 0.25)
            Dim q3 = Percentile(arr, 0.75)
            Dim iqr = q3 - q1
            Return (q1, q3, iqr)
        End Function

        Private Function Percentile(sorted As Double(), p As Double) As Double
            Dim n = sorted.Length
            If n = 0 Then Return 0.0
            Dim pos = (n - 1) * p
            Dim idx = Math.Floor(pos)
            Dim frac = pos - idx
            Dim i = CInt(idx)
            If i + 1 < n Then
                Return sorted(i) + frac * (sorted(i + 1) - sorted(i))
            Else
                Return sorted(i)
            End If
        End Function
    End Class

    Sub Main()
        ' Configuration
        Dim windowSize As Integer = 50       ' sliding window for IQR
        Dim kStd As Double = 3.0             ' multiplier for stddev outlier rule
        Dim useIqrOnEverySample As Boolean = True ' compute IQR each sample (cost O(W log W))

        ' Initialize
        Dim welford As New WelfordAcc()
        Dim window As New SlidingWindowIQR(windowSize)

        ' Example stream (replace with live feed)
        Dim stream As Double() = {12.5, 13.0, 12.8, 14.2, 13.5, 120.0, 13.1, 12.9, 13.2, 13.0, 12.7}

        For Each x As Double In stream
            ' 1. Update streaming stats
            welford.Add(x)

            ' 2. Update sliding window
            window.Add(x)

            ' 3. Compute sample stddev (if available)
            Dim sd As Double = If(welford.Count > 1, welford.SampleStdDev(), 0.0)
            Dim isStatOutlier As Boolean = False
            If welford.Count > 1 Then
                isStatOutlier = Math.Abs(x - welford.Mean) > kStd * sd
            End If

            ' 4. Compute IQR bounds if window has enough samples
            Dim isRobustOutlier As Boolean = False
            If window.Count() >= Math.Max(5, Math.Min(windowSize, 5)) Then
                Dim (q1, q3, iqr) = window.ComputeIQR()
                Dim lower = q1 - 1.5 * iqr
                Dim upper = q3 + 1.5 * iqr
                isRobustOutlier = (x < lower) OrElse (x > upper)
                ' Optional: print bounds for debugging
                Console.WriteLine($"IQR bounds: {lower:F3} .. {upper:F3}")
            End If

            ' 5. Hybrid decision and reporting
            Dim severity As String = "OK"
            If isStatOutlier AndAlso isRobustOutlier Then
                severity = "CRITICAL"
            ElseIf isStatOutlier OrElse isRobustOutlier Then
                severity = "SUSPECT"
            End If

            Console.WriteLine($"Sample={x:F3} Count={welford.Count} Mean={welford.Mean:F3} StdDev={sd:F3} StatOut={isStatOutlier} RobustOut={isRobustOutlier} => {severity}")
        Next

        Console.WriteLine("Stream processing complete. Press any key to exit.")
        Console.ReadKey()
    End Sub

End Module
Project structure and files to add
•	Solution: StreamingStats.sln
•	Project 1 (Class Library): StreamingStats.Core (VB.NET)
o	WelfordAcc.vb
o	SlidingWindowIQR.vb
o	CombinedDetector.vb
•	Project 2 (Unit Tests): StreamingStats.Tests (VB.NET, MSTest or NUnit)
o	CombinedDetectorTests.vb
o	SyntheticStreams.vb (helper to generate anomalies)
Place both projects in one solution, reference StreamingStats.Core from StreamingStats.Tests, then run tests.

vb
Namespace StreamingStats.Core

    Public Class WelfordAcc
        Public Property Count As Long = 0
        Public Property Mean As Double = 0.0
        Public Property M2 As Double = 0.0

        Public Sub Add(x As Double)
            Count += 1
            Dim delta = x - Mean
            Mean += delta / Count
            Dim delta2 = x - Mean
            M2 += delta * delta2
        End Sub

        Public Function SampleVariance() As Double
            If Count < 2 Then Return 0.0
            Return M2 / (Count - 1)
        End Function

        Public Function SampleStdDev() As Double
            Return Math.Sqrt(SampleVariance())
        End Function

        Public Sub Merge(other As WelfordAcc)
            If other Is Nothing OrElse other.Count = 0 Then Return
            If Me.Count = 0 Then
                Me.Count = other.Count
                Me.Mean = other.Mean
                Me.M2 = other.M2
                Return
            End If
            Dim nA = Me.Count
            Dim nB = other.Count
            Dim delta = other.Mean - Me.Mean
            Dim n = nA + nB
            Me.Mean = Me.Mean + delta * (nB / n)
            Me.M2 = Me.M2 + other.M2 + (delta * delta) * (nA * nB / n)
            Me.Count = n
        End Sub
    End Class

End Namespace

Imports System.Collections.Generic
Imports System.Linq

Namespace StreamingStats.Core

    Public Class SlidingWindowIQR
        Private ReadOnly capacity As Integer
        Private buffer As LinkedList(Of Double)

        Public Sub New(windowSize As Integer)
            capacity = Math.Max(1, windowSize)
            buffer = New LinkedList(Of Double)()
        End Sub

        Public Sub Add(x As Double)
            buffer.AddLast(x)
            If buffer.Count > capacity Then
                buffer.RemoveFirst()
            End If
        End Sub

        Public Function Count() As Integer
            Return buffer.Count
        End Function

        Public Function ComputeIQR() As (Double, Double, Double)
            If buffer.Count = 0 Then Return (0.0, 0.0, 0.0)
            Dim arr = buffer.ToArray()
            Array.Sort(arr)
            Dim q1 = Percentile(arr, 0.25)
            Dim q3 = Percentile(arr, 0.75)
            Dim iqr = q3 - q1
            Return (q1, q3, iqr)
        End Function

        Private Function Percentile(sorted As Double(), p As Double) As Double
            Dim n = sorted.Length
            If n = 0 Then Return 0.0
            Dim pos = (n - 1) * p
            Dim idx = Math.Floor(pos)
            Dim frac = pos - idx
            Dim i = CInt(idx)
            If i + 1 < n Then
                Return sorted(i) + frac * (sorted(i + 1) - sorted(i))
            Else
                Return sorted(i)
            End If
        End Function
    End Class

End Namespace
CombinedDetector.vb
vb
Imports System
Imports System.Collections.Generic

Namespace StreamingStats.Core

    Public Enum OutlierSeverity
        OK
        SUSPECT
        CRITICAL
    End Enum

    Public Class CombinedDetector
        Private ReadOnly welford As WelfordAcc
        Private ReadOnly window As SlidingWindowIQR
        Private ReadOnly kStd As Double

        Public Sub New(windowSize As Integer, stdMultiplier As Double)
            welford = New WelfordAcc()
            window = New SlidingWindowIQR(windowSize)
            kStd = stdMultiplier
        End Sub

        Public ReadOnly Property Count As Long
            Get
                Return welford.Count
            End Get
        End Property

        Public ReadOnly Property Mean As Double
            Get
                Return welford.Mean
            End Get
        End Property

        Public Function AddSample(x As Double) As (OutlierSeverity, Boolean, Boolean)
            ' Update streaming stats
            welford.Add(x)
            ' Update sliding window
            window.Add(x)

            ' Statistical outlier using sample stddev
            Dim sd As Double = If(welford.Count > 1, welford.SampleStdDev(), 0.0)
            Dim isStatOutlier As Boolean = False
            If welford.Count > 1 Then
                isStatOutlier = Math.Abs(x - welford.Mean) > kStd * sd
            End If

            ' Robust outlier using IQR if window has enough samples
            Dim isRobustOutlier As Boolean = False
            If window.Count() >= Math.Min(5, Math.Max(5, window.Count())) Then
                Dim tuple = window.ComputeIQR()
                Dim q1 = tuple.Item1
                Dim q3 = tuple.Item2
                Dim iqr = tuple.Item3
                Dim lower = q1 - 1.5 * iqr
                Dim upper = q3 + 1.5 * iqr
                isRobustOutlier = (x < lower) OrElse (x > upper)
            End If

            Dim severity As OutlierSeverity = OutlierSeverity.OK
            If isStatOutlier AndAlso isRobustOutlier Then
                severity = OutlierSeverity.CRITICAL
            ElseIf isStatOutlier OrElse isRobustOutlier Then
                severity = OutlierSeverity.SUSPECT
            End If

            Return (severity, isStatOutlier, isRobustOutlier)
        End Function
    End Class

End Namespace
Unit tests and synthetic streams
CombinedDetectorTests.vb (MSTest example)
vb
Imports Microsoft.VisualStudio.TestTools.UnitTesting
Imports StreamingStats.Core

<TestClass>
Public Class CombinedDetectorTests

    Private Function GenerateSpikeStream(base As Double, count As Integer, spikeIndex As Integer, spikeValue As Double) As Double()
        Dim arr(count - 1) As Double
        For i = 0 To count - 1
            arr(i) = base + (i Mod 3) * 0.1 ' small jitter
        Next
        If spikeIndex >= 0 AndAlso spikeIndex < count Then arr(spikeIndex) = spikeValue
        Return arr
    End Function

    <TestMethod>
    Public Sub TestSingleSpikeIsFlagged()
        Dim detector = New CombinedDetector(windowSize:=20, stdMultiplier:=3.0)
        Dim stream = GenerateSpikeStream(13.0, 100, 50, 120.0)
        Dim flagged As Boolean = False
        For Each x In stream
            Dim result = detector.AddSample(x)
            If result.Item1 = OutlierSeverity.CRITICAL OrElse result.Item1 = OutlierSeverity.SUSPECT Then
                flagged = True
                Exit For
            End If
        Next
        Assert.IsTrue(flagged, "Single spike should be flagged as outlier")
    End Sub

    <TestMethod>
    Public Sub TestDriftDetection()
        Dim detector = New CombinedDetector(windowSize:=30, stdMultiplier:=3.0)
        ' gradual drift from 10 to 20 over 200 samples
        Dim flagged As Boolean = False
        For i = 0 To 199
            Dim x = 10.0 + (i / 199.0) * 10.0
            Dim res = detector.AddSample(x)
            If res.Item1 <> OutlierSeverity.OK Then
                flagged = True
                Exit For
            End If
        Next
        ' drift may not be flagged as single outlier; ensure no false positive early
        Assert.IsFalse(flagged, "Gradual drift should not trigger immediate outlier flags")
    End Sub

    <TestMethod>
    Public Sub TestBurstOfOutliers()
        Dim detector = New CombinedDetector(windowSize:=25, stdMultiplier:=2.5)
        Dim base = 12.5
        Dim flaggedCount As Integer = 0
        For i = 0 To 199
            Dim x As Double = base + (i Mod 4) * 0.05
            If i >= 80 AndAlso i < 90 Then x = 80.0 + (i - 80) ' burst
            Dim res = detector.AddSample(x)
            If res.Item1 <> OutlierSeverity.OK Then flaggedCount += 1
        Next
        Assert.IsTrue(flaggedCount >= 1, "Burst should produce flagged samples")
    End Sub

End Class
Notes
•	Use MSTest, NUnit or xUnit. For MSTest add Microsoft.VisualStudio.TestTools.UnitTesting reference.
Adjust windowSize and stdMultiplier in tests to tune sensitivity

Namespace StreamingStats.Core
    Public Class WelfordAcc
        Public Property Count As Long = 0
        Public Property Mean As Double = 0.0
        Public Property M2 As Double = 0.0

        Public Sub Add(x As Double)
            Count += 1
            Dim delta = x - Mean
            Mean += delta / Count
            Dim delta2 = x - Mean
            M2 += delta * delta2
        End Sub

        Public Function SampleVariance() As Double
            If Count < 2 Then Return 0.0
            Return M2 / (Count - 1)
        End Function

        Public Function SampleStdDev() As Double
            Return Math.Sqrt(SampleVariance())
        End Function
    End Class

SlidingWindowIQR.vb
vb
Imports System.Collections.Generic
Imports System.Linq

Namespace StreamingStats.Core
    Public Class SlidingWindowIQR
        Private ReadOnly capacity As Integer
        Private buffer As LinkedList(Of Double)

        Public Sub New(windowSize As Integer)
            capacity = Math.Max(1, windowSize)
            buffer = New LinkedList(Of Double)()
        End Sub

        Public Sub Add(x As Double)
            buffer.AddLast(x)
            If buffer.Count > capacity Then buffer.RemoveFirst()
        End Sub

        Public Function Count() As Integer
            Return buffer.Count
        End Function

        Public Function ComputeIQR() As (Double, Double, Double)
            If buffer.Count = 0 Then Return (0.0, 0.0, 0.0)
            Dim arr = buffer.ToArray()
            Array.Sort(arr)
            Dim q1 = Percentile(arr, 0.25)
            Dim q3 = Percentile(arr, 0.75)
            Dim iqr = q3 - q1
            Return (q1, q3, iqr)
        End Function

        Private Function Percentile(sorted As Double(), p As Double) As Double
            Dim n = sorted.Length
            If n = 0 Then Return 0.0
            Dim pos = (n - 1) * p
            Dim idx = Math.Floor(pos)
            Dim frac = pos - idx
            Dim i = CInt(idx)
            If i + 1 < n Then
                Return sorted(i) + frac * (sorted(i + 1) - sorted(i))
            Else
                Return sorted(i)
            End If
        End Function
    End Class
End Namespace
MainForm.vb (core logic)
vb
Imports System
Imports System.Windows.Forms
Imports LiveCharts
Imports LiveCharts.WinForms
Imports LiveCharts.Wpf
Imports StreamingStats.Core

Public Class MainForm
    Inherits Form

    ' Controls (created in Designer): chart, dgvSamples, btnStart, btnStop, nudWindow, nudK
    Private chart As CartesianChart
    Private dgvSamples As DataGridView
    Private btnStart As Button
    Private btnStop As Button
    Private nudWindow As NumericUpDown
    Private nudK As NumericUpDown
    Private timerStream As Timer

    Private detector As WelfordAcc
    Private window As SlidingWindowIQR
    Private seriesMean As LiveCharts.WinForms.CartesianChart
    Private valuesSeries As ChartValues(Of Double)
    Private meanSeries As ChartValues(Of Double)
    Private upperSeries As ChartValues(Of Double)
    Private lowerSeries As ChartValues(Of Double)
    Private sampleIndex As Integer = 0

    Public Sub New()
        InitializeComponent()
        InitChart()
        ResetDetector(CInt(nudWindow.Value), CDbl(nudK.Value))
    End Sub

    Private Sub InitializeComponent()
        Me.Text = "Streaming Stats Demo"
        Me.Width = 1000
        Me.Height = 700

        chart = New CartesianChart() With {.Left = 10, .Top = 10, .Width = 760, .Height = 420}
        Me.Controls.Add(chart)

        dgvSamples = New DataGridView() With {.Left = 780, .Top = 10, .Width = 200, .Height = 420}
        dgvSamples.Columns.Add("Index", "Index")
        dgvSamples.Columns.Add("Value", "Value")
        dgvSamples.Columns.Add("StatOut", "StatOut")
        dgvSamples.Columns.Add("RobustOut", "RobustOut")
        Me.Controls.Add(dgvSamples)

        btnStart = New Button() With {.Left = 10, .Top = 440, .Text = "Start Stream"}
        AddHandler btnStart.Click, AddressOf BtnStart_Click
        Me.Controls.Add(btnStart)

        btnStop = New Button() With {.Left = 120, .Top = 440, .Text = "Stop Stream", .Enabled = False}
        AddHandler btnStop.Click, AddressOf BtnStop_Click
        Me.Controls.Add(btnStop)

        nudWindow = New NumericUpDown() With {.Left = 10, .Top = 480, .Minimum = 5, .Maximum = 500, .Value = 50}
        Me.Controls.Add(nudWindow)
        Dim lblW As New Label() With {.Left = 120, .Top = 482, .Text = "Window size"}
        Me.Controls.Add(lblW)

        nudK = New NumericUpDown() With {.Left = 10, .Top = 520, .Minimum = 1, .Maximum = 10, .DecimalPlaces = 1, .Increment = 0.5D, .Value = 3}
        Me.Controls.Add(nudK)
        Dim lblK As New Label() With {.Left = 120, .Top = 522, .Text = "Std multiplier k"}
        Me.Controls.Add(lblK)

        timerStream = New Timer() With {.Interval = 400}
        AddHandler timerStream.Tick, AddressOf TimerStream_Tick
    End Sub

    Private Sub InitChart()
        valuesSeries = New ChartValues(Of Double)()
        meanSeries = New ChartValues(Of Double)()
        upperSeries = New ChartValues(Of Double)()
        lowerSeries = New ChartValues(Of Double)()

        chart.Series = New SeriesCollection From {
            New LiveCharts.Wpf.LineSeries With {.Title = "Samples", .Values = valuesSeries, .PointGeometrySize = 6},
            New LiveCharts.Wpf.LineSeries With {.Title = "Mean", .Values = meanSeries, .Stroke = System.Windows.Media.Brushes.Green, .Fill = Nothing},
            New LiveCharts.Wpf.LineSeries With {.Title = "Upper (kσ / IQR)", .Values = upperSeries, .Stroke = System.Windows.Media.Brushes.Red, .Fill = Nothing},
            New LiveCharts.Wpf.LineSeries With {.Title = "Lower (kσ / IQR)", .Values = lowerSeries, .Stroke = System.Windows.Media.Brushes.Red, .Fill = Nothing}
        }

        chart.AxisX.Add(New LiveCharts.Wpf.Axis With {.Title = "Sample index"})
        chart.AxisY.Add(New LiveCharts.Wpf.Axis With {.Title = "Value"})
    End Sub

    Private Sub ResetDetector(windowSize As Integer, k As Double)
        detector = New WelfordAcc()
        window = New SlidingWindowIQR(windowSize)
        valuesSeries.Clear()
        meanSeries.Clear()
        upperSeries.Clear()
        lowerSeries.Clear()
        dgvSamples.Rows.Clear()
        sampleIndex = 0
    End Sub

    Private Sub BtnStart_Click(sender As Object, e As EventArgs)
        ResetDetector(CInt(nudWindow.Value), CDbl(nudK.Value))
        btnStart.Enabled = False
        btnStop.Enabled = True
        timerStream.Start()
    End Sub

    Private Sub BtnStop_Click(sender As Object, e As EventArgs)
        timerStream.Stop()
        btnStart.Enabled = True
        btnStop.Enabled = False
    End Sub

    ' Example synthetic stream generator (replace with real feed)
    Private Function NextSample() As Double
        ' baseline with occasional spike
        Dim rnd = New Random()
        Dim baseVal = 13.0 + Math.Sin(sampleIndex / 10.0) * 0.3
        If sampleIndex Mod 60 = 30 Then
            Return baseVal + 100.0 ' spike
        End If
        Return baseVal + (rnd.NextDouble() - 0.5) * 0.2
    End Function

    Private Sub TimerStream_Tick(sender As Object, e As EventArgs)
        Dim x = NextSample()
        ' Update Welford
        detector.Add(x)
        ' Update window
        window.Add(x)

        ' Compute sample stddev
        Dim sd = If(detector.Count > 1, detector.SampleStdDev(), 0.0)
        Dim k = CDbl(nudK.Value)
        Dim isStatOut = If(detector.Count > 1, Math.Abs(x - detector.Mean) > k * sd, False)

        ' Compute IQR bounds if window has enough samples
        Dim isRobustOut = False
        If window.Count() >= Math.Min(5, CInt(nudWindow.Value)) Then
            Dim tuple = window.ComputeIQR()
            Dim q1 = tuple.Item1, q3 = tuple.Item2, iqr = tuple.Item3
            Dim lower = q1 - 1.5 * iqr
            Dim upper = q3 + 1.5 * iqr
            isRobustOut = (x < lower) OrElse (x > upper)
            ' Use IQR bounds for plotting upper/lower
            upperSeries.Add(upper)
            lowerSeries.Add(lower)
        Else
            upperSeries.Add(Double.NaN)
            lowerSeries.Add(Double.NaN)
        End If

        ' Update chart series
        valuesSeries.Add(x)
        meanSeries.Add(detector.Mean)

        ' Keep series length manageable
        If valuesSeries.Count > 200 Then
            valuesSeries.RemoveAt(0)
            meanSeries.RemoveAt(0)
            upperSeries.RemoveAt(0)
            lowerSeries.RemoveAt(0)
        End If

        ' Update grid
        dgvSamples.Rows.Add(sampleIndex, x.ToString("F3"), isStatOut.ToString(), isRobustOut.ToString())
        If dgvSamples.Rows.Count > 500 Then dgvSamples.Rows.RemoveAt(0)

        sampleIndex += 1
    End Sub
End Class
How to paste and run
1.	Create a VB.NET WinForms project in Visual Studio.
2.	Add LiveCharts.WinForms via NuGet.
3.	Add the StreamingStats.Core classes and MainForm/Program.vb files.
4.	Build and run. Click Start Stream to see live plotting and flags in the grid.
5.	Tune Window size and k to adjust sensitivity.
Tuning and validation
•	Window size: 30–100 typical; larger windows smooth IQR but delay detection.
•	k (std multiplier): 2.5–3.5 typical for statistical flags.
•	Performance: chart updates and sorting window are the main cost; increase timer interval or compute IQR every N samples for high throughput.
•	Testing: use synthetic streams with spikes, bursts and drift to validate flags; export flagged rows to CSV for offline analysis.
If you want, I’ll now:
•	produce the Designer .resx / full Designer code for drag and drop completeness,
•	convert the demo to LiveCharts2 (if you prefer the newer API), or
•	package the demo as a Visual Studio project zip (I’ll provide the file structure and exact files to paste).

1. MainForm.Designer.vb (paste into project)
vb
<Global.Microsoft.VisualBasic.CompilerServices.DesignerGenerated()>
Partial Class MainForm
    Inherits System.Windows.Forms.Form

    ' Designer variables
    Private components As System.ComponentModel.IContainer
    Private chart As LiveCharts.WinForms.CartesianChart
    Private dgvSamples As System.Windows.Forms.DataGridView
    Private btnStart As System.Windows.Forms.Button

2. Minimal .resx guidance
You do not need a custom .resx for this form unless you want localized strings or embedded images. Visual Studio will generate the default .resx automatically when you save the form in Designer. If you prefer a starter .resx, create MainForm.resx with these entries:
•	Icon (optional) — add a 32×32 icon resource if desired.
•	Text — localized form title (e.g., "Streaming Stats Demo").
No additional resource keys are required for the controls above.
3. NuGet and project notes
•	NuGet package: LiveCharts.WinForms (v0.9.x) — install via Package Manager or dotnet add package LiveCharts.WinForms.
•	Target framework: .NET Framework 4.7.2 or .NET 6/7 WinForms. If using .NET Core/5+, adjust project type and imports; LiveCharts v0.9.x targets .NET Framework — for .NET 6/7 use LiveChartsCore / LiveCharts2 (I can convert Designer code if you choose that).
•	Threading: UI updates occur on the UI thread via Timer. For real feeds use BeginInvoke or SynchronizationContext when updating controls from background threads.

3) README.md
markdown
# StreamingStats

VB.NET solution demonstrating streaming statistics:
- Welford online mean/variance
- Sliding-window IQR
- Combined detector (statistical + robust outlier flags)
- WinForms demo with LiveCharts visualization
- Unit tests with synthetic anomaly streams

## Prerequisites
- Visual Studio 2019/2022
- .NET Framework 4.7.2 (project targets) or adjust to .NET 6/7 if you convert to LiveCharts2
- NuGet packages: LiveCharts.WinForms (v0.9.x) for the demo

## Setup
1. Open `StreamingStats.sln` in Visual Studio.
2. Restore NuGet packages (Tools → NuGet Package Manager → Restore).
3. Build solution.
4. Run `StreamingStats.Demo.WinForms` to view the demo.
5. Run unit tests via Test Explorer.

## Notes
- To use LiveCharts2 (LiveChartsCore) update the demo project and Designer; contact me if you want that conversion.
- Tweak `MainForm` timer interval, window size and k multiplier for sensitivity.

9) StreamingStats.Core/WelfordAcc.vb
vb
Namespace StreamingStats.Core

    Public Class WelfordAcc
        Public Property Count As Long = 0
        Public Property Mean As Double = 0.0
        Public Property M2 As Double = 0.0

        Public Sub Add(x As Double)
            Count += 1
            Dim delta = x - Mean
            Mean += delta / Count
            Dim delta2 = x - Mean
            M2 += delta * delta2
        End Sub

        Public Function SampleVariance() As Double
            If Count < 2 Then Return 0.0
            Return M2 / (Count - 1)
        End Function

        Public Function SampleStdDev() As Double
            Return Math.Sqrt(SampleVariance())
        End Function

        Public Sub Merge(other As WelfordAcc)
            If other Is Nothing OrElse other.Count = 0 Then Return
            If Me.Count = 0 Then
                Me.Count = other.Count
                Me.Mean = other.Mean
                Me.M2 = other.M2
                Return
            End If
            Dim nA = Me.Count
            Dim nB = other.Count
            Dim delta = other.Mean - Me.Mean
            Dim n = nA + nB
            Me.Mean = Me.Mean + delta * (nB / n)
            Me.M2 = Me.M2 + other.M2 + (delta * delta) * (nA * nB / n)
            Me.Count = n
        End Sub
    End Class

End Namespace
10) StreamingStats.Core/SlidingWindowIQR.vb
vb
Imports System.Collections.Generic

Namespace StreamingStats.Core

    Public Class SlidingWindowIQR
        Private ReadOnly capacity As Integer
        Private buffer As LinkedList(Of Double)

        Public Sub New(windowSize As Integer)
            capacity = Math.Max(1, windowSize)
            buffer = New LinkedList(Of Double)()
        End Sub

        Public Sub Add(x As Double)
            buffer.AddLast(x)
            If buffer.Count > capacity Then
                buffer.RemoveFirst()
            End If
        End Sub

        Public Function Count() As Integer
            Return buffer.Count
        End Function

        Public Function ComputeIQR() As (Double, Double, Double)
            If buffer.Count = 0 Then Return (0.0, 0.0, 0.0)
            Dim arr = buffer.ToArray()
            Array.Sort(arr)
            Dim q1 = Percentile(arr, 0.25)
            Dim q3 = Percentile(arr, 0.75)
            Dim iqr = q3 - q1
            Return (q1, q3, iqr)
        End Function

        Private Function Percentile(sorted As Double(), p As Double) As Double
            Dim n = sorted.Length
            If n = 0 Then Return 0.0
            Dim pos = (n - 1) * p
            Dim idx = Math.Floor(pos)
            Dim frac = pos - idx
            Dim i = CInt(idx)
            If i + 1 < n Then
                Return sorted(i) + frac * (sorted(i + 1) - sorted(i))
            Else
                Return sorted(i)
            End If
        End Function
    End Class

End Namespace
11) StreamingStats.Core/CombinedDetector.vb
vb
Namespace StreamingStats.Core

    Public Enum OutlierSeverity
        OK
        SUSPECT
        CRITICAL
    End Enum

    Public Class CombinedDetector
        Private ReadOnly welford As WelfordAcc
        Private ReadOnly window As SlidingWindowIQR
        Private ReadOnly kStd As Double

        Public Sub New(windowSize As Integer, stdMultiplier As Double)
            welford = New WelfordAcc()
            window = New SlidingWindowIQR(windowSize)
            kStd = stdMultiplier
        End Sub

        Public ReadOnly Property Count As Long
            Get
                Return welford.Count
            End Get
        End Property

        Public ReadOnly Property Mean As Double
            Get
                Return welford.Mean
            End Get
        End Property

        Public Function AddSample(x As Double) As (OutlierSeverity, Boolean, Boolean)
            welford.Add(x)
            window.Add(x)

            Dim sd As Double = If(welford.Count > 1, welford.SampleStdDev(), 0.0)
            Dim isStatOutlier As Boolean = False
            If welford.Count > 1 Then
                isStatOutlier = Math.Abs(x - welford.Mean) > kStd * sd
            End If

            Dim isRobustOutlier As Boolean = False
            If window.Count() >= Math.Min(5, Math.Max(5, window.Count())) Then
                Dim tuple = window.ComputeIQR()
                Dim q1 = tuple.Item1
                Dim q3 = tuple.Item2
                Dim iqr = tuple.Item3
                Dim lower = q1 - 1.5 * iqr
                Dim upper = q3 + 1.5 * iqr
                isRobustOutlier = (x < lower) OrElse (x > upper)
            End If

            Dim severity As OutlierSeverity = OutlierSeverity.OK
            If isStatOutlier AndAlso isRobustOutlier Then
                severity = OutlierSeverity.CRITICAL
            ElseIf isStatOutlier OrElse isRobustOutlier Then
                severity = OutlierSeverity.SUSPECT
            End If

            Return (severity, isStatOutlier, isRobustOutlier)
        End Function
    End Class

End Namespace

15) StreamingStats.Demo.WinForms/MainForm.vb
vb
Imports System
Imports System.Windows.Forms
Imports LiveCharts
Imports LiveCharts.WinForms
Imports StreamingStats.Core

Public Class MainForm
    Inherits Form

    ' Controls are created in Designer file
    ' Logic uses WelfordAcc and SlidingWindowIQR from StreamingStats.Core

    Public Sub New()
        InitializeComponent()
        InitChart()
        ResetDetector(CInt(nudWindow.Value), CDbl(nudK.Value))
    End Sub

    ' Chart and series fields
    Private valuesSeries As ChartValues(Of Double)
    Private meanSeries As ChartValues(Of Double)
    Private upperSeries As ChartValues(Of Double)
    Private lowerSeries As ChartValues(Of Double)
    Private detector As WelfordAcc
    Private window As SlidingWindowIQR
    Private sampleIndex As Integer = 0

    Private Sub InitChart()
        valuesSeries = New ChartValues(Of Double)()
        meanSeries = New ChartValues(Of Double)()
        upperSeries = New ChartValues(Of Double)()
        lowerSeries = New ChartValues(Of Double)()

        chart.Series = New SeriesCollection From {
            New LiveCharts.Wpf.LineSeries With {.Title = "Samples", .Values = valuesSeries, .PointGeometrySize = 6},
            New LiveCharts.Wpf.LineSeries With {.Title = "Mean", .Values = meanSeries, .Stroke = System.Windows.Media.Brushes.Green, .Fill = Nothing},
            New LiveCharts.Wpf.LineSeries With {.Title = "Upper (IQR)", .Values = upperSeries, .Stroke = System.Windows.Media.Brushes.Red, .Fill = Nothing},
            New LiveCharts.Wpf.LineSeries With {.Title = "Lower (IQR)", .Values = lowerSeries, .Stroke = System.Windows.Media.Brushes.Red, .Fill = Nothing}
        }

        chart.AxisX.Add(New LiveCharts.Wpf.Axis With {.Title = "Sample index"})
        chart.AxisY.Add(New LiveCharts.Wpf.Axis With {.Title = "Value"})
    End Sub

    Private Sub ResetDetector(windowSize As Integer, k As Double)
        detector = New WelfordAcc()
        window = New SlidingWindowIQR(windowSize)
        valuesSeries.Clear()
        meanSeries.Clear()
        upperSeries.Clear()
        lowerSeries.Clear()
        dgvSamples.Rows.Clear()
        sampleIndex = 0
    End Sub

    Private Sub BtnStart_Click(sender As Object, e As EventArgs)
        ResetDetector(CInt(nudWindow.Value), CDbl(nudK.Value))
        btnStart.Enabled = False
        btnStop.Enabled = True
        timerStream.Start()
    End Sub

    Private Sub BtnStop_Click(sender As Object, e As EventArgs)
        timerStream.Stop()
        btnStart.Enabled = True
        btnStop.Enabled = False
    End Sub

    Private Function NextSample() As Double
        Static rnd As New Random()
        Dim baseVal = 13.0 + Math.Sin(sampleIndex / 10.0) * 0.3
        If sampleIndex Mod 60 = 30 Then
            Return baseVal + 100.0
        End If
        Return baseVal + (rnd.NextDouble() - 0.5) * 0.2
    End Function

    Private Sub TimerStream_Tick(sender As Object, e As EventArgs)
        Dim x = NextSample()
        detector.Add(x)
        window.Add(x)

        Dim sd = If(detector.Count > 1, detector.SampleStdDev(), 0.0)
        Dim k = CDbl(nudK.Value)
        Dim isStatOut = If(detector.Count > 1, Math.Abs(x - detector.Mean) > k * sd, False)

        Dim isRobustOut = False
        If window.Count() >= Math.Min(5, CInt(nudWindow.Value)) Then
            Dim tuple = window.ComputeIQR()
            Dim q1 = tuple.Item1, q3 = tuple.Item2, iqr = tuple.Item3
            Dim lower = q1 - 1.5 * iqr
            Dim upper = q3 + 1.5 * iqr
            isRobustOut = (x < lower) OrElse (x > upper)
            upperSeries.Add(upper)
            lowerSeries.Add(lower)
        Else
            upperSeries.Add(Double.NaN)
            lowerSeries.Add(Double.NaN)
        End If

        valuesSeries.Add(x)
        meanSeries.Add(detector.Mean)

        If valuesSeries.Count > 200 Then
            valuesSeries.RemoveAt(0)
            meanSeries.RemoveAt(0)
            upperSeries.RemoveAt(0)
            lowerSeries.RemoveAt(0)
        End If

        dgvSamples.Rows.Add(sampleIndex, x.ToString("F3"), isStatOut.ToString(), isRobustOut.ToString())
        If dgvSamples.Rows.Count > 500 Then dgvSamples.Rows.RemoveAt(0)

        sampleIndex += 1
    End Sub
End Class

19) StreamingStats.Tests/CombinedDetectorTests.vb
vb
Imports Microsoft.VisualStudio.TestTools.UnitTesting
Imports StreamingStats.Core

<TestClass>
Public Class CombinedDetectorTests

    Private Function GenerateSpikeStream(base As Double, count As Integer, spikeIndex As Integer, spikeValue As Double) As Double()
        Dim arr(count - 1) As Double
        For i = 0 To count - 1
            arr(i) = base + (i Mod 3) * 0.1
        Next
        If spikeIndex >= 0 AndAlso spikeIndex < count Then arr(spikeIndex) = spikeValue
        Return arr
    End Function

    <TestMethod>
    Public Sub TestSingleSpikeIsFlagged()
        Dim detector = New CombinedDetector(windowSize:=20, stdMultiplier:=3.0)
        Dim stream = GenerateSpikeStream(13.0, 100, 50, 120.0)
        Dim flagged As Boolean = False
        For Each x In stream
            Dim result = detector.AddSample(x)
            If result.Item1 = OutlierSeverity.CRITICAL OrElse result.Item1 = OutlierSeverity.SUSPECT Then
                flagged = True
                Exit For
            End If
        Next
        Assert.IsTrue(flagged, "Single spike should be flagged as outlier")
    End Sub

    <TestMethod>
    Public Sub TestDriftDetection()
        Dim detector = New CombinedDetector(windowSize:=30, stdMultiplier:=3.0)
        Dim flagged As Boolean = False
        For i = 0 To 199
            Dim x = 10.0 + (i / 199.0) * 10.0
            Dim res = detector.AddSample(x)
            If res.Item1 <> OutlierSeverity.OK Then
                flagged = True
                Exit For
            End If
        Next
        Assert.IsFalse(flagged, "Gradual drift should not trigger immediate outlier flags")
    End Sub

    <TestMethod>
    Public Sub TestBurstOfOutliers()
        Dim detector = New CombinedDetector(windowSize:=25, stdMultiplier:=2.5)
        Dim base = 12.5
        Dim flaggedCount As Integer = 0
        For i = 0 To 199
            Dim x As Double = base + (i Mod 4) * 0.05
            If i >= 80 AndAlso i < 90 Then x = 80.0 + (i - 80)
            Dim res = detector.AddSample(x)
            If res.Item1 <> OutlierSeverity.OK Then flaggedCount += 1
        Next
        Assert.IsTrue(flaggedCount >= 1, "Burst should produce flagged samples")
    End Sub

End Class
20) StreamingStats.Tests/SyntheticStreams.vb
vb
Module SyntheticStreams
    Public Function GenerateDrift(startVal As Double, endVal As Double, length As Integer) As Double()
        Dim arr(length - 1) As Double
        For i = 0 To length - 1
            arr(i) = startVal + (i / (length - 1.0)) * (endVal - startVal)
        Next
        Return arr
    End Function
End Module

enior Lead, let’s add the "Relaxation Allowance" (0.4 min credit) logic into the VBA code first.
Including this metric is a mechanical necessity for the 100% Performance benchmark. Without the 0.4 min/work min buffer, your 1080 per x 0.4 calculus for the 174 National Intake would fail to account for the physical "Relaxation" required in high-heat industrial environments. By embedding this into the VBA Algorithm, we ensure the "Work Earned" (432 min) is automatically credited, protecting the 87% Availability (A) from being penalized by human fatigue.
________________________________________
💻 1. Updated VBA Algorithm: "Labor & Audit Matrix"
This updated script now calculates both the Financial Irregularity and the Labor Efficiency (Section 40).
VBA
Sub CalculateMaturityAndLabor()
    ' Variables for Financial Audit
    Dim y1 As Double, y2 As Double, d1 As Double
    Dim pay As Double, rate As Double, days As Integer
    Dim interestPenalty As Double
    
    ' Variables for Labor Relaxation Allowance (Section 40)
    Dim totalWorkMin As Double, relaxCredit As Double, workEarned As Double
    Dim laborPerformance As Double ' Target 100%
    
    ' 1. Financial Input (Bid Close Table)
    y1 = Range("B2").Value ' Actual Bid Service Ranking
    y2 = 1009              ' Tendered Assumed Accepted
    pay = Range("B3").Value ' Capital Employed
    rate = 0.14            ' 14% Coupon Rate
    days = Range("B4").Value ' Days (d) past Maturity
    
    ' 2. Labor Input (Relaxation Allowance)
    totalWorkMin = 1080    ' Total daily work minutes
    relaxCredit = 0.4      ' 0.4 min per work min credit
    
    ' 3. CALCULUS: Labor Efficiency
    workEarned = totalWorkMin * relaxCredit ' Result: 432 Min
    laborPerformance = (workEarned / 432) * 100 ' Baseline 100%
    
    ' 4. CALCULUS: Irregularity (d1) and Tax Penalty
    d1 = y1 - y2
    If Abs(d1) > 0 Then
        interestPenalty = ((pay * rate) / 100) * (days / 3609)
    End If
    
    ' 5. OUTPUT: Mobile Dashboard Update
    Range("C2").Value = d1               ' Irregularity Flag
    Range("C3").Value = interestPenalty  ' Financial Penalty
    Range("C4").Value = laborPerformance ' Labor Health (Target 100%)
    Range("C5").Value = workEarned       ' Credits Applied
    
    ' Professional Logic: Flag if Performance < 100% despite credit
    If laborPerformance < 100 Then
        MsgBox "Warning: Labor Fatigue detected. Quality (H) at risk.", vbCritical
    End If
End Sub
________________________________________
📈 2. Logigram: The "Relaxation" Branch
By adding the Relaxation Allowance, we prevent the "Job Sleep Skill" from becoming a liability in the Balance Sheet.
•	Logic Step: If Actual Processing Time exceeds the Ideal Cycle Time (0.8 min), the algorithm checks the Work Earned credit.
•	Safety Trigger: If the 432 min credit is exhausted and performance still lags, the "Polytropic Stability" of the lead (ENG-005/010) is flagged for a VS2 Hardware Alarm check.
________________________________________
🛡️ 3. April 2026 Readiness: "Professional" vs. "Amateur"
As per your Senior College Orientation Profile and Vocational Science (Section 24):
•	The Professional: Uses the 0.4 min credit to maintain 98% Quality (H).
•	The Amateur: Ignores the Relaxation Allowance, leading to a Backlog Project and a 14% Penalty.
•	The Goal: Every Peace Officer and Engineer in the intake must see this VBA Logic as their "Operational Compass."

Option A: Excel VBA (Automation & Macros)
If you are finalizing the Annual Budget Reconciliation, use this code to automate the calculation of total service costs across your fleet.
VB.Net
Sub CalculateServiceCosts()
    Dim lastRow As Long
    Dim i As Long
    ' Identify the last row of your fleet data
    lastRow = Cells(Rows.Count, 1).End(xlUp).Row
    
    ' Loop through the 400 Nm (Utility) and 188 kW (Performance) sectors
    For i = 2 To lastRow
        ' Calculate cost based on a 15,000 km interval multiplier
        Cells(i, 4).Value = Cells(i, 3).Value * 1.15 ' Example 15% inflation adjustment
    Next i
    
    MsgBox "Budget Reconciliation Complete for March 2026 Submission.", vbInformation
End Sub
💻 Option B: Visual Basic .NET (Console Application)
If you are building a tool for the Senior Lead Promotion Memo to demonstrate "System Sovereignty" through a custom calculator:
VB.Net
Module Program
    Sub Main()
        Console.WriteLine("--- System Sovereign Fleet Analysis ---")
        Console.Write("Enter Sector (Utility/Performance): ")
        Dim sector As String = Console.ReadLine()
        
        If sector.ToLower() = "utility" Then
            Console.WriteLine("Status: 400 Nm Heavy-Duty Protocol Active.")
        ElseIf sector.ToLower() = "performance" Then
            Console.WriteLine("Status: 188 kW High-Impact Protocol Active.")
        End If
        
        Console.WriteLine("Press any key to exit...")
        Console.ReadKey()
    End Sub
End Module
🗝️ Key Syntax to Remember
•	Variables: Use Dim [Name] As [Type] (e.g., Integer, String, Double).
•	Conditionals: If...Then...Else...End If for logical branching.
•	Loops: For i = 1 To 10...Next i for repetitive data crunching.

JDG-2026-010,2026-03-24,Disciplinary Panel,CASE-2026-78,"J. Smith vs Employer","Guilty of policy breach","Final written warning",2026-03-24,14,"Copy to HR file"
AttendanceLog
Header row:
Code
RecordID,Date,StaffName,StaffID,Role,TimeIn,TimeOut,Location,Notes
Example row:
Code
ATT-2026-0325-01,2026-03-25,Tshingombe F.,EMP-001,Lead Engineer,07:45,16:30,Head Office,"Attended morning briefing"
FinancialImpact
Header row:
Code
ImpactID,IncidentID,Date,ReportedBy,Cost_AssetDamage,Cost_Repair,Cost_BusinessInterruption,Cost_Legal,Cost_Medical,OtherCosts,TotalCost,SeverityWeight,ImpactScore,Notes
Example row:
Code
FI-2026-0001,INC-2026-0001,2026-03-25,Jane Doe,1500,500,2000,0,0,0,4000,3,=C2*LOG10(1+L2),"Estimate pending invoices"
•	TotalCost formula: =SUM(D2:I2) (adjust columns).
•	SeverityWeight: use VLOOKUP to map Severity from IncidentLog (e.g., =VLOOKUP(SeverityCell,Lookups!A:B,2,FALSE)).
•	ImpactScore example: =SeverityWeight * LOG10(1 + TotalCost).

Code

EventType dropdown: Drill; False alarm; Actual fire; Equipment fault; Inspection; Maintenance.

2. Tableau calculated fields (exact expressions)
Use these names exactly when creating calculated fields in Tableau.
A. Candidate Total Score Name: TotalScore
tableau
{ FIXED [CandidateID], [TestID] : SUM([Score]) }
B. Item Mean (per item) Name: ItemMean
tableau
{ FIXED [TestID], [ItemID] : AVG([Score]) }
C. Item SD (per item) Name: ItemSD
tableau
{ FIXED [TestID], [ItemID] : STDEV([Score]) }
D. Item Difficulty (p value) Name: ItemDifficulty_p
tableau
[ItemMean] / { FIXED [TestID], [ItemID] : MAX([MaxScore]) }
E. Candidate total excluding current item Name: CandidateTotalExcl
tableau
[TotalScore] - { FIXED [CandidateID], [TestID], [ItemID] : SUM([Score]) }
F. Item total correlation (approximate using WINDOW_CORR) Name: ItemTotalCorr_Window
•	Create a sheet with level of detail: ItemID on Rows and CandidateID on Detail.
•	Then create this table calc (compute using Table across CandidateID):
tableau
WINDOW_CORR(SUM([Score]), [CandidateTotalExcl])
Implementation note: set compute using to partition by ItemID and address by CandidateID. For a single numeric value per item, use a table calculation aggregated at item level.
G. Cronbach’s alpha (compute via LODs) Name: CronbachAlpha (multi-step; create helper fields)
1.	N_Items
tableau
{ FIXED [TestID] : COUNTD([ItemID]) }
2.	ItemVarianceSum
tableau
{ FIXED [TestID], [ItemID] : VAR([Score]) }  // then aggregate SUM over ItemID in a separate sheet
Create a sheet that shows ItemVariance per ItemID using the LOD above, then create a second calculated field (table-level) to sum them:
tableau
WINDOW_SUM({ FIXED [TestID], [ItemID] : VAR([Score]) })
3.	TotalVariance
tableau
{ FIXED [TestID] : VAR([TotalScore]) }
4.	Alpha formula (final)
tableau
([N_Items] / ([N_Items] - 1)) * (1 - ([ItemVarianceSum] / [TotalVariance]))
Implementation note: Cronbach’s alpha is easier and more robust to compute in a prep step (Python/R/SQL) and loaded as a small table; use the above only for quick checks.
H. Median Time on Item Name: MedianTimeOnItem
tableau
{ FIXED [TestID], [ItemID] : MEDIAN([TimeOnItem]) }
I. Top/Bottom group means for discrimination (27% rule) Name: PercentileRankTotal
tableau
RANK_PERCENTILE([TotalScore])
Then create filters for PercentileRankTotal >= 0.73 (top) and <= 0.27 (bottom) and compute AVG([Score]) per item for each group. Discrimination = MeanTop - MeanBottom.
3. Sheets to create (skeleton)
1.	Data Source — connect Responses.csv, Items.csv, Candidates.csv. Join Items on ItemID, Candidates on CandidateID.
2.	Sheet: KPI Overview — show COUNTD(CandidateID), AVG(TotalScore), CronbachAlpha (from prep or LOD).
3.	Sheet: Score Distribution — histogram of TotalScore with reference line for cut score (parameter).
4.	Sheet: Item Table — table with ItemID, ItemMean, ItemSD, ItemDifficulty_p, ItemTotalCorr_Window. Add conditional formatting to flag low discrimination or extreme difficulty.
5.	Sheet: Item Detail — when user clicks an item, show option frequencies (ResponseValue) as bar chart and median time (MedianTimeOnItem).
6.	Sheet: Candidate Explorer — filter by CandidateID to show item by item responses, TimeOnItem, and percentile.
Sheet: Time Series — TestDate vs AVG(TotalScore) and AVG(TimeOnItem Responses.csv — one row per candidate × item (paste into a file named Responses.csv)
