vb
Sub CreateLandReformDeck()
    Dim pres As Presentation
    Dim s As Slide
    Dim shp As Shape
    Dim leftPos As Single, topPos As Single, w As Single, h As Single
    Dim stages As Variant, i As Integer
    Dim colors As Variant
    Dim cht As Shape
    Dim chartDataWorkbook As Object
    Dim chartSeries As Object

    ' Create new presentation
    Set pres = Application.Presentations.Add

    ' --- Slide 1: Title (already created by default) ---
    Set s = pres.Slides(1)
    s.Layout = ppLayoutTitle
    s.Shapes.Title.TextFrame.TextRange.Text = "Land Reform & Governance Framework"
    s.Shapes.Placeholders(2).TextFrame.TextRange.Text = "Réforme foncière & cadre de gouvernance"

    ' --- Slide 2: Financial Flow / Timeline ---
    Set s = pres.Slides.Add(2, ppLayoutBlank)
    ' Left column: bilingual bullets
    leftPos = 20
    topPos = 30
    w = 360
    h = 300
    Set shp = s.Shapes.AddTextbox(Orientation:=msoTextOrientationHorizontal, _
        Left:=leftPos, Top:=topPos, Width:=w, Height:=h)
    shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Font.Name = "Calibri"
    shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Font.Size = 11
    shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Text = "Budget Allocation & Procurement / Allocation budgétaire & passation de marchés" & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & _
        "• Multi-year budget planning for land reform programs / Planification budgétaire pluriannuelle pour les programmes de réforme foncière" & vbCrLf & _
        "• Transparent bid award protocols and supply chain oversight / Protocoles transparents d'attribution des marchés et supervision de la chaîne d'approvisionnement" & vbCrLf & _
        "• Cost tracking dashboards for audit readiness / Tableaux de suivi des coûts pour la préparation aux audits"

    ' Right column: timeline bar
    leftPos = 400
    topPos = 80
    w = 480
    h = 120
    stages = Array(Array("Planning", "Planification"), Array("Procurement", "Passation"), Array("Execution", "Exécution"), Array("Audit", "Audit"))
    colors = Array(RGB(0, 112, 192), RGB(0, 176, 80), RGB(255, 153, 51), RGB(192, 0, 0))

    Dim segLeft As Single, segWidth As Single
    segLeft = leftPos
    segWidth = w / UBound(stages) + 1

    For i = 0 To UBound(stages)
        Set shp = s.Shapes.AddShape(Type:=msoShapeRectangle, Left:=segLeft, Top:=topPos, Width:=segWidth - 6, Height:=h)
        shp.Fill.ForeColor.RGB = colors(i)
        shp.Line.Visible = msoFalse
        shp.TextFrame.VerticalAnchor = msoAnchorMiddle
        shp.TextFrame.TextRange.ParagraphFormat.Alignment = ppAlignCenter
        shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Font.Color.RGB = RGB(255, 255, 255)
        shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Font.Bold = msoTrue
        shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Font.Size = 12
        shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Text = stages(i)(0) & " / " & stages(i)(1)
        segLeft = segLeft + segWidth
    Next i

    ' Add connecting arrow below timeline
    Set shp = s.Shapes.AddLine(BeginX:=leftPos + 10, BeginY:=topPos + h + 10, EndX:=leftPos + w - 10, EndY:=topPos + h + 10)
    shp.Line.EndArrowheadStyle = msoArrowheadTriangle
    shp.Line.Weight = 2

    ' Caption
    Set shp = s.Shapes.AddTextbox(Orientation:=msoTextOrientationHorizontal, Left:=20, Top:=topPos + h + 30, Width:=860, Height:=40)
    shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Font.Name = "Calibri"
    shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Font.Size = 10
    shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Text = "Strategic budgeting and transparent procurement drive reform success. / La budgétisation stratégique et les passations transparentes assurent le succès de la réforme."

    ' --- Slide 3: Community Impact / Pie Chart ---
    Set s = pres.Slides.Add(3, ppLayoutBlank)
    ' Left column: bilingual bullets
    leftPos = 20
    topPos = 30
    w = 360
    h = 220
    Set shp = s.Shapes.AddTextbox(Orientation:=msoTextOrientationHorizontal, _
        Left:=leftPos, Top:=topPos, Width:=w, Height:=h)
    shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Font.Name = "Calibri"
    shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Font.Size = 11
    shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Text = "Equity, Tenure, and Rights / Équité, tenure et droits" & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & _
        "• Community engagement in reform design and rollout / Implication communautaire dans la conception et le déploiement de la réforme" & vbCrLf & _
        "• Protection of tenure rights and dispute resolution / Protection des droits de tenure et mécanismes de résolution des conflits" & vbCrLf & _
        "• Monitoring equity outcomes across regions / Suivi des résultats en matière d’équité dans les différentes régions"

    ' Right column: pie chart
    leftPos = 420
    topPos = 60
    w = 420
    h = 300
    Set cht = s.Shapes.AddChart2(Style:=201, XlChartType:=xlPie, Left:=leftPos, Top:=topPos, Width:=w, Height:=h)
    ' Access chart data workbook
    Set chartDataWorkbook = cht.Chart.ChartData.Workbook
    chartDataWorkbook.Activate

    ' Write data into the embedded workbook
    With chartDataWorkbook.Worksheets(1)
        .Cells.Clear
        .Range("A1").Value = "Stakeholder"
        .Range("B1").Value = "Share"
        .Range("A2").Value = "Government / Gouvernement"
        .Range("B2").Value = 25
        .Range("A3").Value = "Community / Communauté"
        .Range("B3").Value = 30
        .Range("A4").Value = "Legal / Juridique"
        .Range("B4").Value = 20
        .Range("A5").Value = "Technical / Technique"
        .Range("B5").Value = 15
        .Range("A6").Value = "Oversight / Supervision"
        .Range("B6").Value = 10
    End With

    ' Refresh chart to use new data
    cht.Chart.SetSourceData Source:=chartDataWorkbook.Worksheets(1).Range("A1:B6")
    cht.Chart.HasTitle = False
    cht.Chart.ChartArea.Format.Line.Visible = msoFalse

    ' Format pie slices with distinct colors
    Dim ps As Point
    Dim sliceColors As Variant
    sliceColors = Array(RGB(0, 112, 192), RGB(255, 204, 0), RGB(146, 208, 80), RGB(255, 153, 51), RGB(192, 0, 0))
    For i = 1 To 5
        Set ps = cht.Chart.SeriesCollection(1).Points(i)
        ps.Format.Fill.ForeColor.RGB = sliceColors(i - 1)
    Next i

    ' Add legend with bilingual labels
    cht.Chart.HasLegend = True
    cht.Chart.Legend.Position = xlLegendPositionRight

    ' Close the chart data workbook (keeps data embedded)
    chartDataWorkbook.Application.Quit

    ' Caption
    Set shp = s.Shapes.AddTextbox(Orientation:=msoTextOrientationHorizontal, Left:=20, Top:=topPos + h + 10, Width:=820, Height:=40)
    shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Font.Name = "Calibri"
    shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Font.Size = 10
    shp.TextFrame.TextRange.Text = "Inclusive reforms foster security and fairness for all stakeholders. / Des réformes inclusives favorisent la sécurité et l'équité pour toutes les parties prenantes."

    ' Final: show first slide
    pres.Slides(1).Select
    MsgBox "Mini deck created: 3 slides (Title, Financial Flow timeline, Community Impact pie chart).", vbInformation
End Sub
If you want next
•	I can provide a VBA variant for Excel (draw timeline with shapes on a worksheet and create the pie chart there).
•	Or I can adapt this macro to export each slide as a high resolution PNG (requires small code additions). Which would you like?
Options comparison
Option	Output	Best for	Effort to run	Customizability
VBA for Excel	Timeline drawn on a worksheet + pie chart in Excel	Users who want editable visuals inside Excel for data tweaks and printing	Low — paste macro into Excel and run	High — shapes and chart data live in Excel for easy edits
Export slides as high res PNG	Individual high resolution PNG files of each slide	Ready to use images for handouts, web, or embedding in other docs	Low–Medium — small macro addition to export after deck creation	Medium — images are fixed; regenerate to change visuals
Recommendation
If you plan to adjust numbers or labels frequently or hand the file to finance/analytics teams, choose VBA for Excel. If you need finalized, print quality images for distribution or embedding, choose export as PNG.
Sub Audit_174_Intake()
    Dim i As Integer
    Dim lastRow As Long
    Dim missingCount As Integer
    
    ' Initialize parameters for the National Grid
    lastRow = Sheets("174_Intake_Master").Cells(Rows.Count, 1).End(xlUp).Row
    missingCount = 0
    
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    
    For i = 2 To 174 + 1 ' Header + 174 National Intake
        ' Logic Gate: Check if Competency Score (Column C) is empty
        If IsEmpty(Cells(i, 3).Value) Then
            Cells(i, 3).Interior.Color = vbRed ' Flag the "Fault"
            missingCount = missingCount + 1
        Else
            Cells(i, 3).Interior.Color = xlNone ' Clear the "Grid"
        End If
    Next i
    
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True
    
    ' Final Commissioning Report
    If missingCount = 0 Then
        MsgBox "System Synchronized: All 174 Operators are Audit-Ready.", vbInformation, "Dr. Tshitadi: Lead Engineer"
    Else
        MsgBox "Warning: " & missingCount & " Data Mismatches detected in the Grid.", vbExclamatation, "Logic Fault Detected"
    End If
End Sub
________________________________________
2. The "Bilingual Certificate Generator" (Batch Print)
If you need to generate the individual Commissioning Certificates we drafted earlier, this logic automates the "Mail Merge" directly within Excel.
VBA
Sub Generate_Commissioning_Certificates()
    Dim wsData As Worksheet
    Dim wsCert As Worksheet
    Dim i As Integer
    
    Set wsData = Sheets("174_Intake_Master")
    Set wsCert = Sheets("Certificate_Template")
    
    For i = 2 To 175 ' Loop through 174 Junior Operators
        ' Map Data to the Template
        wsCert.Range("B5").Value = wsData.Cells(i, 1).Value ' Name
        wsCert.Range("B7").Value = wsData.Cells(i, 2).Value ' SAQA/NQF ID
        
        ' Trigger Print-to-PDF (Automated Handover)
        wsCert.ExportAsFixedFormat Type:=xlTypePDF, _
            Filename:="C:\Certificates\Commissioning_" & wsData.Cells(i, 1).Value & ".pdf"
    Next i
    
    MsgBox "174 Certificates have been Digitally Commissioned.", vbInformation, "Handover Protocol Complete"
End Sub
VBA
Function Authenticate_Lead_Engineer() As Boolean
    Dim inputPass As String
    Dim masterPass As String
    
    ' Set your secure password for the March 31st Commissioning
    masterPass = "DrTshitadi2026" 
    
    inputPass = InputBox("Enter Lead Engineer Authentication Code:", "National Grid Security Access")
    
    If inputPass = masterPass Then
        Authenticate_Lead_Engineer = True
    Else
        MsgBox "Access Denied: Unauthorized Command Attempt.", vbCritical, "Security Breach"
        Authenticate_Lead_Engineer = False
    End If
End Function VBA
Sub EMERGENCY_DATA_PURGE()
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim confirmMsg As VbMsgBoxResult
    
    ' Double-Gate Security Check
    confirmMsg = MsgBox("WARNING: This will permanently ERASE all 174 National Intake data. Proceed?", _
                        vbCritical + vbYesNo, "EMERGENCY SELF-DESTRUCT")
    
    If confirmMsg = vbYes Then
        ' Second Authentication Gate
        If Not Authenticate_Lead_Engineer() Then Exit Sub
        
        Application.ScreenUpdating = False
        
        ' Loop through all sheets and clear everything but the headers
        For Each ws In ThisWorkbook.Worksheets
            ws.Cells.ClearContents ' Wipe the data
            ws.Cells.ClearFormats  ' Wipe the metadata
        Next ws
        
        ' Clear the Clipboard and Memory
        Application.CutCopyMode = False
        
        Application.ScreenUpdating = True
        
        MsgBox "System Purge Complete. Grid Zeroed.", vbInformation, "Protocol: Secure Shutdown"
        
        ' Optional: Close the workbook without saving changes to the blank state
        ' ThisWorkbook.Close SaveChanges:=True 
    End If
End Sub
